2a3(29): sems/ stong gsal nam mkha' lta bur bsgom/ a har a/ kun tu snang ni 'gro rnams la/ tshad med bzhoni bskyed kyi 'd lngas snod bcud sbyang par bsgom/ aM 
2a4(29): pur pa ya/ rgyu mchog 'd dang yig 'bru la/ sngags dang phyag rgyas gsal gdab nas/ bdag dang dkyil 'khor bum pa la/ gnal yas bdag dang lha lthar bskyed/ hUM 
2a5(29): rar bu/ lan gsum bdza/ te rin chen dbal kyi gnal yag ni/ gu gsum mcing nag zla gam dmar/ thabs zhes nyi zla' ra ba la/ ye zhes gu chad rin chen / 
2b1(29): sdang / dbyings kyi hing ghi caMd 'bram brtan/ glong gi ra brtsigs rang phyogs la/ mkha' yi ya gad tsen kha gdang / pad 'og phyogs mtshams zar tshogs/ rlung g.sab gzha' 
2b2(29): tshen dar bu chad/ sgo bzhi tshad med phyogs kyi 'od// zla gam cig bzhi steng bzhin gsal/ 'od zer tsha tshar brgyad 'pres/ zangs lhcags me chu dmar nag khor/ sngags dang phyogs 
2b3(29): mtshams 'phres pa ni/ bs oM a pur pa pa / bso oM pa sur pa 'du / bs oM a thun nyi lo yo he rag sha pa pud trang / sa bon rgyu las bskyed pa yi/ rin chen dbal kyi 
2b4(29): gzhal yas khang / gcan lnga nyi zla pad ma dang / drigs pa lha bdud gdan stengs su / bse las 'bar ba'i skur gsal ba/ dbal gss sngam pa khri rgyal mkha' 'gying la/ sku 
2b5(29): gsung thugs sbyor yum dang 'khor/ sku mdog phyag mtshan gdan thabs brjid/ 'jig rten drag po'i phyag rgya bsgom/ bs dbang sdrag 'bar ba'i gzhal yas su/ seng gi glang chen 
2b6(29): rta 'byug khyung / drigs pa nyi zla p rna bcas/ lha rnams bzhugs pa'i gdan du 'brul/ bso oM a thun nyi lo yo spungs so thad de/ sad ge gya nom hrig gi rgyun/ bso bskal pa / 
3a1(29): me ltar 'bar ba'i gsas mkhar nas/ dbal gss sngam pa khri rgyal mkha' 'gying ba/ s+dzu 'hrul gsung dang tsho 'brul thugs kyi lha/ thabs la dgyes pa'i rngam mo / 
3a2(29): srid pa'i yum/ yab yum sgo ma sprul pa'i 'khor bcas rnams/ bs cha ha la drag po'i sgra s+drzogs shing / de bzhin me ltar 'bar ba'i gsas mkhar 'dir/ ma mo bdu btsan / 
3a3(29): dbang du srud pa'i phyir/ gnhen rab mtha dang dpung la spyan 'dren na/ mkha' la sprin gtib lta bu gshegs su gsol/ bso oM a thun nyi lo yog sungs so cad do mu ye ha ra ra yo / 
3a4(29): dza/ bso bon nyid dbyings nas sku bzhengs pa'i/ dbal gss sngam pa khro rgyal mkha' 'gying kha/ sku gsung thugs mchog yab yum 'khor bcas rnams/ bdag nyid ting 'dzin / 
3a5(29): stobs las sprul pa'i/ khro mchog dbal gsas yab yum 'khor bcas rnams/ gnyis med don gyis brnyan par bzhugs su gsol/ bso oM a thun nyi lo yo spungs so thad do/ 
3a6(29): brig go sad di rag ryten du rhyun/ bso zhi ba'i ngang las khros pa'i dbal 'bar ba/ dbal gss sngam pa lha rgod gtso mchog sku gsung thugs/ khro mchog 'dus pa'i sku la phyag 
3b1(29): 'tshal lo// nam mkha'i dbyings nas snang srid mdzod 'dzin cing / gnyis med don gyi shes rab thabs la nyen/ rngam mo sred pa'i yum la phyag 'tshal bstod/ dbyar dgun ston 
3b2(29): dbyed bsgyur ba'i s+dzu 'bhrul can/ zhu rgyas smin bsdud thabs la mkhas pa yi/ sgo sung rgyal mo yum la phyag 'tshal lo// sku gsung thugs mchog gtso las sprul pa yi/ gang
3b3(29): la cis 'dul thabs kyi thugs rje can/ khro rgyal sprul pa'i tshogs la phyag 'tshal lo// bs oM a thun nye lo yon spungs so thad do/ sad de khang la rko pung rgyun/ bso oM pa 
3b4(29): thun nye lo yo spungs so thad do/ sad do mu slus in ting hun/ bs oM a thun nye lo yo spungs so thad de/ sad do ne thun khri seg rhun/ kye gsas mkhar ye shes lha rnams bdag 
3b5(29): la dgongs su gsol/ sgrub ghen bdag la rang rig ye zhes ma ldan pas/ ma rig ma rtogs log rtogs 'khrul dbang gi/ bskal pa'i gong nas dus 'di yan chad du/ ye zhes 
3b6(29): spyan can khyed kyi bka' zhon nas/ thugs nyid ngang la mi 'da' mnyam nyid sku / rang sems dag pas dam tshig gtser len na/ ma rig ma rtogs log rtogs 'khrul pa yis/ 
4a1(29): / b/ bka' dang dam la 'das pa mtsol lo bshags/ gzu lum ra tshod tom tshol tshed yid rnams/ ye shes spyan can khyed la bzod par gsol/ mi 'chab dang pa'i 
4a2(29): sems kyis skyabs su mche/ dug gsum sku gsung thugs mchog ma rtogs pas/ las spyod ma dag dge sdig 'tshol bar spyad/ sku gsung thugs kyi lha la mthol lo bshags/ 
4a3(29): 'byung ba zad med yum gyi ba ga la/ de ltar ma rtogs rgyu lus don du gnyer/ ba g.yum gyis klong du mtsol lo bshags/ snang srid 'khor lo thabs kyi bsgyur ba la/ de ltar ma rtog 
4a4(29): dus dang rtag tu bzung / sgo sung rgyal mo yum la mtsol lo bshags/ byung csher sna tshogs rang bzhin med pa la/ de ltar ma gyur nyon mongs rang khar zhir/ khro rgyal sprul pa'i tshogs 
4a5(29): la mtsol lo bshags/ gyad dmag rgyal chen gtsa rigs lha mgon dang / ma mo bdu btsan dregs pa bathu rtsal can/ khyed kyi tha tshig bdag gis bzhes pa la/ de ltar ma 
4a6(29): rtogs mchod pa lo zlur 'das/ dam can sung ma'i tshogs btsol lo bshags/ mthol bshags phul nas tshangs pa rtsal du gsol/ bs oM a thun nye lo yo spungs so thad do/ 
4b1(29): sad do rko phung u drug gha' ya ni/ bswo oM a thun nye lo yo spungs so thad do/ sad do ago u drug gha' ya ni/ bswo oM a thun nyi lo yo spungs so thad do/ sad de khri seg u / 
4b2(29): dug gzha' ya ni/ bso mkha' kglong dbyings kyis sprul pa la/ stong gsum stong gi 'jig rten kun/ gzhal yas lha ru rag snang pa/ bgegs zhes bya ba med na yang / rtog yid / 
4b3(29): 'khrul pa'i blo byung nas/ mchod la brlam pa'i bar tshod bgegs/ rdul phran bzhin du brlag par bya'o// bso o a thun nyi lo yong spungs so thad d/ tho y hrig gishag dul nan/ 
4b4(29): de nas gtor ma 'brul lo/ bs 'bru gtsang bcud sdus 'ban bshos rgyan ldan la/ dkar ma ra sha khrag zla dgu'i brgyan/ stong gsum bcud bstim dgongs pas byin rlabs nas/ 
4b5(29): 'dod dgu kun ldan zad med longs spyod 'di/ ye zhes khro tshogs rnams la mchod pa 'brul/ thugs rjes byin gyis rlobs la bzhes su gsol/ bso o bong ngor rang zad bin kha 
4b6(29): thim mo// de nas khrag 'brul lo// bs khams gsum 'gro drug rtsad nas bcad nas kyang / sha khrag rus pa dmar gyi rgya mtsho la/ dam s+dzas dmar gyi mchod par bzhes su / 
5a1(29): ggol/ bso mo hri' gting bmu dang ra'dod bcam go// dena lan mchod 'brul lo// b'o mi gsu 'bran bdu rtsi b'o/ b'i dbal gas sngam pa ce rgyal / 
5a2(29): sku gsung thugs/ rngam mo yum chen sred pa bde sgrol ma/ yab yum sprul pa'i 'khor dang bcas pa la/ g.su 'brang bdud rtsi sman kyi mchod par 'brul/ mnyes rab dam pa'i / 
5a3(29): mchog dang ldan nas kyang / tshe dbang mthu yi dngos grub bdag la stsol/ bs o g.su 'brang bdud rtsi dang ra sad de kha thun no// zhu rgyas smin sud sgo ba rgyal mo la/ gsu 'brang / 
5a4(29): bdud rtsi sman kyi mchod par 'brul/ mnyes rab dam pa'i mchog dang ldan nas kyang / tshe dbang mthu yi dngos grub bdag la stsol/ bs o nhung 'brang ting bu dang ra kha tsam mo// 
5a5(29): khro rgyal spul pa po nya'i tshogs rnams la/ gsu 'brang bdud rtsi sman kyi mchod par 'brul/ mnyes rab dam pa'i mchog dang ldan nas kyang / tshe dbang mthu yi dngos grub bdag 
5a6(29): la stsol/ bso o nyung 'brang ting mur dang ra kha thim no// gyad dang dmag dpon ther zugs rgyal chen la/ g.yu 'brang bdud rtsi sman kyi mchod par 'brul/ mnyes rab dam pa'i 
5b1(29): mchog dang ldan nas kyang / tshe dbang mthu yi dngos grub bdag la stsol/ bso oM nyung 'brang ting mur dang ra sad de kha thim mo// ma mo bdud btsan dregs pa bka' nyan la/ g.yu 
5b2(29): 'brang bdud rtsi sman kyi mchod par 'brul/ mnyes rab dam pa'i mchog dang ldan nas kyang / tshe dbang mthu yi dngos grub bdag la stsol/ bs oM nung 'brang ting mu dang ra kha tsam / 
5b3(29): mo// de nas dngos grub blang ngo // bs dbal gsas sngam pa bdud rtsi sku'i lha/ khro gtum brjid pa sku'i dngos grub srtsol/ bs oM a thun nye lo yo spungs so thad do/ bso mu khyung pra

6a1(29): snyan/ thub kyi phyogs nas mtshod 'brul ma/ lum shag mdzes pa'i bar bya shans/ lho'i phyogs nas mtchod 'brul ma/ re hag gsugyi drel bu ldags/ lho shar / 
6a2(29): mtshams nas mchod 'brul ma/ tshul shag gser gyi gsu 'brang sku/ byang shar mtshams nas mchod 'brul ma/ rgya shag me tog ha lo gsung / byang nub mtshams nas mchod /

7a1(29): drigs pa dbang du bsdu ru gsol/ de nas phyag rgya sku bstid bskul pa ni/ bso ma g.yo ma 'jigs con gyi dbyings klong na/ phye dang nang med tsho 'drul gzhal yas / 
7a2(29): hang / rmengs gnhi 'khyams phyogs ya gd gur tog rgyas/ sgo bzni thags byu bglang re thags shrogs nag/ gsas mkhar gnal yas che la phyag 'tshal bstod/ nye zla d+ra /

8a1(29): kbyengs la tlags nyid khros pa'i stobs chen la/ dpal gs sngam pa gri rgyal btha' 'byeng ba/ me bzad bu dg phyag kyang bco brgyad te/ sgu ni 'jig byed /

9b6(29): a thun nye lo yo thun spungs so thad de thun/ hte raga ge du gran la thun byo thun b+yo/ rni rtsi gran la phrig gi thun b+yo/ kher drim gran la hrig gi thun +ho/ sha 'bal gran la

10a4(29): phyi gung rgyal nam mkha'i mdzod 'dzin ma/ yi gshen gtsug pud sku la spul tsam na/ bzang za ring btsun lha mo dar gyi yum/ gsas mkhar rgyas pa'i gtso mo mdzad tsam / 
10a5(29): na/ thugs rje byams ma skye 'gro gso ba'i ma/ lha rgod thig pa'i phrol yum mdzad tsam na/ srid pa'i rgyal mo gzhan kyi 'gran zla med/ mkha' 'gying lha'i gs yum mdzad
